He helps kids progress through the Adventure using just the keys they have learned. \r\n\r\nPacked with Motivation\r\nKids are motivated to learn new keys, pass typing tests and complete challenges to free Mickey and his friends from the enchantment. Games can be played with just the keys they have learned so far, or with all the keys on the keyboard. \r\n\r\nAdventure Settings\r\nThere are a lot of choices on Typelandia.
